                    <strong>
                     Australian resident
                    </strong>
                    if you:
                    <ul>
                     <li>
                      are an Australian or New Zealand citizen; or
                     </li>
                     <li>
                      are an Australian permanent resident; or
                     </li>
                     <li>
                      hold a permanent Australian humanitarian visa.
                     </li>
                    </ul>
                   </div>
                   <div id="international-info-content">
                    You are considered an
                    <strong>
                     international student
                    </strong>
                    if you:
                    <ul>
                     <li>
                      do not fit any of the above criteria; and
                     </li>
                     <li>
                      hold a temporary visa (or are seeking to apply for one).
                     </li>
                    </ul>

                     <a href="https://immi.homeaffairs.gov.au/visas/getting-a-visa/visa-listing/student-500">
                      Department of Home Affairs
                     </a>

       <div class="container">
        <div class="pane-content">
         <div class="entity entity-bean bean-key-selling-points clearfix">
          <div class="content">
           <div class="paragraphs-items paragraphs-items-field-ksp paragraphs-items-field-ksp-full paragraphs-items-full">
            <div class="field field-name-field-ksp field-type-paragraphs field-label-hidden">
             <div class="field-items">
              <div class="field-item even">
               <div class="ksp-component theme-1 heading">
                <h2>
                 THE NEW WAY TO DO UNI
                </h2>
                <div class="ds-1col entity entity-paragraphs-item paragraphs-item-ksps view-mode-full clearfix">
                 <div class="paragraphs-items paragraphs-items-field-ksps paragraphs-items-field-ksps-full paragraphs-items-full">
                  <div class="field field-name-field-ksps field-type-paragraphs field-label-hidden">
                   <div class="field-items">
                    <div class="field-item even">
                     <span class="ksp-component__icon">
                      <img class="ksp-component__icon-svg" src="https://www.vu.edu.au/sites/default/files/ksp1-award-winning-block-40px.svg"/>
                     </span>
                     <div class="ksp-component__content">
                      <span class="ksp-component__title">
                       Award-winning VU Block Model
                      </span>
                      <span class="ksp-component__body">
                       <p>
                        Greater focus, more support and proven success with
                        <a href="/study-at-vu/why-choose-vu/vu-block-model">
                         VUâ€™s Block Model
                        </a>
                       </p>
                      </span>
                     </div>
                    </div>
                    <div class="field-item odd">
                     <span class="ksp-component__icon">
                      <img class="ksp-component__icon-svg" src="https://www.vu.edu.au/sites/default/files/aus-first.svg"/>
                     </span>
                     <div class="ksp-component__content">
                      <span class="ksp-component__title">
                       No.1 for employability
                      </span>
                      <span class="ksp-component__body">
                       <p>
                        Australiaâ€™s
                        <a href="/about-vu/news-events/news/vu-now-no-1-in-australia-for-employability">
                         top university for Employability Skills
                        </a>
                        (2020)
                       </p>
                      </span>
                     </div>
                    </div>
                    <div class="field-item even">
                     <span class="ksp-component__icon">
                      <img class="ksp-component__icon-svg" src="https://www.vu.edu.au/sites/default/files/ksp2-star-top-2-percent.svg"/>
                     </span>

       </div>
       <div class="col-sm-10 col-md-11">
        <h3 class="footer-aoc-title">
         <a href="/about-us/vision-mission/acknowledgement-of-country">
          Acknowledgement of country
         </a>
        </h3>
        <p class="footer-aoc-message">
         Victoria University acknowledges, recognises and respects the Ancestors, Elders and families of the Boonwurrung, Wadawurrung and Wurundjeri of the Kulin who are the traditional owners of University land in Victoria, and the Gadigal and Guring-gai of the Eora Nation who are the traditional owners of University land in Sydney.
        </p>
